united kingdom high court [SEP] the united kingdom high court declared illegal a variety of interest-rate swap transactions and options deals between a london borough council and commercial banks .
london [SEP] the united kingdom high court declared illegal a variety of interest-rate swap transactions and options deals between a london borough council and commercial banks .

new york stock exchange [SEP] dot system -- the `` designated order turnaround '' system was launched by the new york stock exchange in march 1976 , to offer automatic , high-speed order processing .
superdot [SEP] a faster version , the superdot , was launched in 1984 .
superdot [SEP] used by program traders and others to zip orders into the exchange , superdot handles about 80 % of all orders entered at the exchange .
s & p [SEP] indexing -- many investors , mainly institutions , follow an investment strategy of buying and holding a mix of stocks to match the performance of a broad stock-market barometer such as the s & p 500 .
chicago mercantile exchange [SEP] the most common program-trading vehicles are futures contracts on standard & poor 's 500-stock index -lrb- traded on the chicago mercantile exchange -rrb- ; the major market index , a 20-stock index that mimics the dow jones industrial average -lrb- traded on the chicago board of trade -rrb- ; and the s & p 100 options -lrb- traded on the chicago board options exchange , and based on 100 stocks selected from the s & p 500 -rrb- .
